Dev is aggressively punting issues from D5 that are not high severity. 
However, QA should make sure that no critical bugs are punted.  Zimbra is 
concentrating on:



·         Customer support case issues

·         VMW issues

·         Major usability issues (especially with DF/CF)

·         Regressions

·         Severity = Major+

·         High votes issues (which doesn’t really apply to 8.0, since it is 
not yet released)



All others are low priority.



So, next week, I want the QA engineers to go through the “found in 8.0 but 
not targeted for D5” to make sure any severe issues are targeted correctly. 
Hopefully the list will be quite short.  I’ll send out an email next Monday.



-Matt







From: globaladmin@testdomain.com
Sent: Thursday, June 21, 2012 2:11 PM
To: globaladmin@testdomain.com
Subject: zcs 8 triage




Hey guys I ran the ZCS -> Iron Maiden search and still see about 800 items. 
Are you working on punting from this list?

If I run the ZCS -> D5 no target milestone I get around 530 (2nd list 
below).

I talked to Jon and we both feel that we should be punting bugs that we 
don't plan to fix to Not Committed.

Those we feel we'd fix in JudasPriest should get marked JudasPriest.  This 
way we keep IronMaiden

to the list of bugs that we will fix in D5 (ZCS 8 GA) and only customer 
reported or critical issues

will be brought back from Not Committed or JudasPriest for maintenance/patch 
releases of 8.x
